===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product\product-popup-create.component\pages\product-popup-create.component.ts =====
import {
  Component,
  EventEmitter,
  Output,
  OnInit,
  ChangeDetectorRef,
} from '@angular/core';
import { trigger, transition, style, animate } from '@angular/animations';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { finalize } from 'rxjs/operators';
import { ProductService } from '../../product.component/services/product-service';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import { ProductCategory } from '../../../product-category/models/product-category-response.model';
import { ProductCategoryService } from '../../../product-category/services/product-category.service';
import { NzSelectModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/select';
import { NzFormModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/form';

@Component({
  selector: 'product-popup-create',
  standalone: true,
  imports: [CommonModule, FormsModule, NzSelectModule, NzFormModule],
  templateUrl: './product-popup-create.component.html',
  animations: [
    trigger('fadeInOut', [
      transition(':enter', [
        style({ opacity: 0, transform: 'scale(0.95)' }),
        animate('300ms ease-out', style({ opacity: 1, transform: 'scale(1)' })),
      ]),
      transition(':leave', [
        animate(
          '200ms ease-in',
          style({ opacity: 0, transform: 'scale(0.90)' })
        ),
      ]),
    ]),
  ],
})
export class ProductPopupCreateComponent implements OnInit {
  name: string = '';
  productCategoryId: string = '';
  unit: number = 6;
  salePrice: number = 0;
  imageUrl: string = '';
  description: string = '';
  categories: ProductCategory[] = [];

  searchTerm: string = '';
  filteredCategories: ProductCategory[] = [];
  showDropdown: boolean = false;

  @Output() closePopupCreate = new EventEmitter<void>();
  @Output() create = new EventEmitter<void>();

  isClosing: boolean = false;
  isSaving: boolean = false;
  isSerialTracked: boolean = false;

  constructor(
    private productService: ProductService,
    private categoryService: ProductCategoryService,
    private toastr: ToastrService,
    private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef
  ) {}

  ngOnInit(): void {
    this.loadCategories();
  }

  private loadCategories(): void {
    this.categoryService.GetAll().subscribe({
      next: (res) => {
        this.categories = (res.ProductCategories || []).filter(
          (cat) => cat.IsActive == false
        );
        this.filteredCategories = [...this.categories];
        console.log('Categories loaded:', this.categories);
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: () => {
        this.toastr.error('KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ load loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m');
      },
    });
  }
  filterCategories(): void {
    const term = this.searchTerm.toLowerCase();
    this.filteredCategories = this.categories.filter((cat) =>
      cat.Name.toLowerCase().includes(term)
    );

    const matched = this.categories.find(
      (cat) => cat.Name.toLowerCase() === term
    );
    if (!matched) this.productCategoryId = '';
  }

  selectCategory(cat: ProductCategory): void {
    this.productCategoryId = cat.Id;
    this.searchTerm = cat.Name;
    this.showDropdown = false;
  }

  onBlur(): void {
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.showDropdown = false;

      const match = this.categories.find((cat) => cat.Name === this.searchTerm);
      if (!match) {
        this.productCategoryId = '';
        this.searchTerm = '';
      }
    }, 200);
  }

  close(): void {
    this.closePopupCreate.emit();
  }

  onSubmit(): void {
    if (this.isSaving) return;

    if (!this.productCategoryId) {
      this.toastr.warning('Vui lÃ²ng chá»n loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m');
      return;
    }

    this.isSaving = true;
    this.productService
  .CreateProduct(
    this.name,
    this.productCategoryId,
    this.unit,
    this.salePrice,
    this.imageUrl,
    this.description || '',
    this.isSerialTracked 
  )
      .pipe(finalize(() => (this.isSaving = false)))
      .subscribe({
        next: () => {
          this.toastr.success('Táº¡o má»›i sáº£n pháº©m thÃ nh cÃ´ng');
          this.create.emit();
          this.close();
        },
        error: (err) => {
          const apiMessage = err.error?.Message;
          let userMessage = 'Cáº­p nháº­t tháº¥t báº¡i';

          if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.VALIDATION.MESSAGE.ALREADY_EXIST') {
            userMessage = 'Sáº£n pháº©m Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng';
          } else if (apiMessage) {
            userMessage = apiMessage;
          }
          this.toastr.error(userMessage);
        },
      });
  }
}

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product\product-popup-search.component\product-popup-search.component.ts =====
import { Product } from './../product.component/models/product-response.model';
import { InventoryDetail } from './../../inventory-receipt/models/warehouse-receipt-detail.model';
import {
  ChangeDetectorRef,
  Component,
  EventEmitter,
  Input,
  OnInit,
  Output,
} from '@angular/core';
import { ProductService } from '../product.component/services/product-service';
import { ProductResponse } from '../product.component/models/product-response.model';
import { map } from 'rxjs';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import { NzTableComponent, NzTableModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/table';
import { UnitTextPipe } from '../../../shared/pipes/unit-text-pipe';
import { NzCheckboxModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/checkbox';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { NzIconModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/icon';
import { NzPaginationComponent } from 'ng-zorro-antd/pagination';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';

@Component({
  selector: 'product-popup-search',
  imports: [
    CommonModule,
    FormsModule,
    NzTableComponent,
    UnitTextPipe,
    NzCheckboxModule,
    NzTableModule,
    NzIconModule,
    NzPaginationComponent,
  ],
  templateUrl: './product-popup-search.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./product-popup-search.component.scss'],
})
export class ProductPopupSearchComponent implements OnInit {
  @Input() shouldDisableProduct: boolean = true;
  @Input() ProductQuantity: boolean = true;
  @Input() existingProducts: string[] = [];
  @Output() closePopup = new EventEmitter<void>();
  @Output() selectProducts = new EventEmitter<InventoryDetail[]>();
  isClosing = false;
  isDark = false;
  listOfData: Product[] = [];
  originalData: Product[] = [];
  listOfCurrentPageData: Product[] = [];
  setOfCheckedId = new Set<string>();
  checked = false;
  indeterminate = false;
  pageIndex = 1;
  pageSize = 10;
  totalCount = 0;
  searchKeyword = '';
  isLoading = false;
  isMobile = window.innerWidth <= 768;
  disabledProductIds = new Set<string>();
  constructor(
    private productService: ProductService,
    private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef,
    private toastr: ToastrService
  ) {}

  ngOnInit(): void {
    this.fetchData();
  }

  onSaveSelectedProducts(): void {
    const selectedInventoryDetails: InventoryDetail[] = this.originalData
      .filter(
        (p) =>
          this.setOfCheckedId.has(p.Id) &&
          (!this.shouldDisableProduct || !this.disabledProductIds.has(p.Id))
      )
      .map((p) => ({
        Id: p.Id,
        ProductId: p.Id,
        ProductName: p.Name,
        ProductCode: p.Code,
        Unit: p.Unit,
        Quantity: 0,
        SalePrice: p.SalePrice,
        InventoryReceiptId: '',
        Available: p.Available,
      }));

    if (selectedInventoryDetails.length === 0) {
      this.toastr.warning('KhÃ´ng cÃ³ sáº£n pháº©m há»£p lá»‡ Ä‘Æ°á»£c chá»n!');
      this.closePopup.emit();
      return;
    }

    this.selectProducts.emit(selectedInventoryDetails);
    this.closePopup.emit();
  }

  close() {
    this.isClosing = true;
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.closePopup.emit();
    }, 800);
  }
  onPageChange(page: number): void {
    this.pageIndex = page;
    this.fetchData(this.pageIndex, this.pageSize);
  }

  fetchData(
    pageIndex: number = this.pageIndex,
    pageSize: number = this.pageSize
  ): void {
    this.isLoading = true;

    this.productService
      .SearchProduct(this.searchKeyword || null, 1000, 1, false) // láº¥y Ä‘á»§ data
      .subscribe({
        next: (res) => {
          const existingIds = new Set(this.existingProducts);

          // Bá» sáº£n pháº©m Ä‘Ã£ cÃ³
          let filtered = (res.Products || []).filter(
            (p) => !existingIds.has(p.Id)
          );

          if (!this.ProductQuantity) {
            filtered = filtered.filter((p) => (p.Available ?? 0) > 0);
          }

          // âœ… LÆ°u toÃ n bá»™ danh sÃ¡ch Ä‘Ã£ filter Ä‘á»ƒ dÃ¹ng láº¡i khi save
          this.originalData = filtered;

          // Paging á»Ÿ frontend
          const start = (pageIndex - 1) * pageSize;
          const end = start + pageSize;
          this.listOfData = filtered.slice(start, end);

          this.totalCount = filtered.length;

          this.listOfCurrentPageData = [...this.listOfData];
          this.isLoading = false;
          this.cdr.detectChanges();
        },
        error: () => {
          this.isLoading = false;
        },
      });
  }

  onSearch(): void {
    this.pageIndex = 1;
    this.searchKeyword = this.searchKeyword.trim();
    this.fetchData(this.pageIndex, this.pageSize);
  }

  listOfSelection = [
    {
      text: 'Chá»n táº¥t cáº£ hÃ ng',
      onSelect: () => {
        this.onAllChecked(true);
      },
    },
    {
      text: 'Chá»n hÃ ng cháºµn',
      onSelect: () => {
        this.listOfCurrentPageData.forEach((data, index) =>
          this.updateCheckedSet(data.Id, index % 2 !== 0)
        );
        this.refreshCheckedStatus();
      },
    },
    {
      text: 'Chá»n hÃ ng láº»',
      onSelect: () => {
        this.listOfCurrentPageData.forEach((data, index) =>
          this.updateCheckedSet(data.Id, index % 2 === 0)
        );
        this.refreshCheckedStatus();
      },
    },
  ];

  updateCheckedSet(id: string, chk: boolean) {
    chk ? this.setOfCheckedId.add(id) : this.setOfCheckedId.delete(id);
  }
  onItemChecked(id: string, chk: boolean) {
    this.updateCheckedSet(id, chk);
    this.refreshCheckedStatus();
  }
  onAllChecked(val: boolean) {
    this.listOfCurrentPageData.forEach((item) => {
      //   if (!this.disabledProductIds.has(item.Id)) {
      this.updateCheckedSet(item.Id, val);
      // }
    });
    this.refreshCheckedStatus();
  }

  onCurrentPageDataChange(data: readonly Product[]): void {
    this.listOfCurrentPageData = [...data];
  }

  refreshCheckedStatus() {
    this.checked = this.listOfCurrentPageData.every((i) =>
      this.setOfCheckedId.has(i.Id)
    );
    this.indeterminate =
      this.listOfCurrentPageData.some((i) => this.setOfCheckedId.has(i.Id)) &&
      !this.checked;
  }
  trackById(index: number, item: Product): string {
    return item.Id;
  }
}

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product\product-popup-update.component\product-popup-update.component.ts =====
import { Product } from './../product.component/models/product-response.model';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import {
  ChangeDetectorRef,
  Component,
  EventEmitter,
  Input,
  OnInit,
  Output,
} from '@angular/core';
import { trigger, transition, style, animate } from '@angular/animations';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { NzSelectModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/select';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import { ProductService } from '../product.component/services/product-service';
import { finalize } from 'rxjs';
import { ProductCategoryService } from '../../product-category/services/product-category.service';
import { ProductCategory } from '../../product-category/models/product-category-response.model';

@Component({
  selector: 'product-popup-update',
  standalone: true,
  imports: [CommonModule, FormsModule, NzSelectModule],
  templateUrl: './product-popup-update.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./product-popup-update.component.scss'],
  animations: [
    trigger('fadeInOut', [
      transition(':enter', [
        style({ opacity: 0, transform: 'scale(0.95)' }),
        animate('300ms ease-out', style({ opacity: 1, transform: 'scale(1)' })),
      ]),
      transition(':leave', [
        animate(
          '200ms ease-in',
          style({ opacity: 0, transform: 'scale(0.95)' })
        ),
      ]),
    ]),
  ],
})
export class ProductPopupUpdateComponent implements OnInit {
  @Input() data!: Product;
  @Output() closePopup = new EventEmitter<void>();
  @Output() update = new EventEmitter<void>();

  categories: ProductCategory[] = [];
  filteredCategories: ProductCategory[] = [];
  searchTerm: string = '';
  showDropdown: boolean = false;
  isClosing = false;
  isSaving = false;

  constructor(
    private productService: ProductService,
    private categoryService: ProductCategoryService,
    private toastr: ToastrService,
    private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef
  ) {}

  ngOnInit(): void {
    if (this.data) {
      this.searchTerm = this.data.ProductCategoryName || '';
    }
    this.loadCategories();
  }

  private loadCategories(): void {
    this.categoryService.GetAll().subscribe({
      next: (res) => {
        this.categories = (res.ProductCategories || []).filter(
          (cat) => cat.IsActive
        );
        this.filteredCategories = [...this.categories];
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: () => {
        this.toastr.error('KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ load loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m');
      },
    });
  }

  filterCategories(): void {
    const term = this.searchTerm.toLowerCase();
    this.filteredCategories = this.categories.filter((cat) =>
      cat.Name.toLowerCase().includes(term)
    );

    const matched = this.categories.find(
      (cat) => cat.Name.toLowerCase() === term
    );
    if (!matched || matched.Name !== this.searchTerm) {
      this.data.ProductCategoryId = '';
    }
  }

  selectCategory(cat: ProductCategory): void {
    this.data.ProductCategoryId = cat.Id;
    this.searchTerm = cat.Name;
    this.showDropdown = false;
  }

  onBlur(): void {
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.showDropdown = false;

      const match = this.categories.find((cat) => cat.Name === this.searchTerm);
      if (!match) {
        this.data.ProductCategoryId = '';
        this.searchTerm = '';
      }

      this.cdr.detectChanges();
    }, 200);
  }

  close() {
    this.isClosing = true;
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.closePopup.emit();
      this.isClosing = false;
      this.cdr.detectChanges();
    }, 200);
  }

  onSubmit() {
    if (this.isSaving) return;
    console.log('Submitting data:', this.data.ProductCategoryId);
    this.isSaving = true;
    console.log('catID 2:', this.data.ProductCategoryId);

    this.productService
      .UpdateProduct(
        this.data.Id,
        this.data.RowVersion,
        this.data.ProductCategoryId,
        this.data.Name.trim(),
        this.data.Unit,
        this.data.IsActive,
        this.data.SalePrice ?? 0, 
        this.data.ImageUrl,
        this.data.SupplierId,
        this.data.Description.trim() || ''
      )
      .pipe(
        finalize(() => {
          setTimeout(() => {
            this.isSaving = false;
            this.cdr.detectChanges();
          });
        })
      )
      .subscribe({
        next: () => {
          this.toastr.success('Cáº­p nháº­t thÃ nh cÃ´ng');
          this.update.emit();
          this.close();
        },
        error: (err) => {
          const apiMessage = err.error?.Message;
          let userMessage = 'Cáº­p nháº­t tháº¥t báº¡i';

          if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.APP_MESSAGE.DATA_NOT_EXIST') {
            userMessage = 'Sáº£n pháº©m khÃ´ng tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng.';
          } else if (
            apiMessage === 'BACKEND.VALIDATION.MESSAGE.NOT_VALID_ROWVERSION'
          ) {
            userMessage =
              'Dá»¯ liá»‡u Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Æ°á»£c cáº­p nháº­t bá»Ÿi ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng khÃ¡c. Vui lÃ²ng táº£i láº¡i trang Ä‘á»ƒ tiáº¿p tá»¥c.';
          } else if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.APP_MESSAGE.DATA_DUPLICATE') {
            userMessage = 'TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i.';
          } else if (apiMessage) {
            userMessage = apiMessage;
          }
          this.toastr.error(userMessage);
        },
      });
  }
}

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product\product.component\pages\product.component.ts =====
import {
  ChangeDetectorRef,
  Component,
  HostListener,
  OnInit,
} from '@angular/core';
import { NzFloatButtonModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/float-button';
import { NzModalModule, NzModalService } from 'ng-zorro-antd/modal';
import { HeaderCommonComponent } from '../../../shared/header-common.component/header-common.component';
import { RouterModule } from '@angular/router';
import { NzIconModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/icon';
import { BottomMenuComponent } from '../../../shared/bottom-menu.component/bottom-menu.component';
import { NzButtonModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/button';
import { NzCheckboxModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/checkbox';
import { NzTableModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/table';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { CommonModule, DatePipe } from '@angular/common';
import { Product } from '../models/product-response.model';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import { ProductService } from '../services/product-service';
import { Location } from '@angular/common';
import * as XLSX from 'xlsx';
import saveAs from 'file-saver';
import { ProductPopupCreateComponent } from '../../product-popup-create.component/pages/product-popup-create.component';
import { ProductPopupUpdateComponent } from '../../product-popup-update.component/product-popup-update.component';
import { UnitTextPipe } from '../../../../shared/pipes/unit-text-pipe';
import { NzDropDownModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/dropdown';
import { NzMenuModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/menu';
import { MenuComponent } from '../../../shared/menu.component/menu.component';
import { NzPaginationModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/pagination';

@Component({
  selector: 'product',
  standalone: true,
  imports: [
    CommonModule,
    FormsModule,
    NzTableModule,
    NzCheckboxModule,
    NzButtonModule,
    BottomMenuComponent,
    NzIconModule,
    RouterModule,
    HeaderCommonComponent,
    NzModalModule,
    NzFloatButtonModule,
    ProductPopupCreateComponent,
    ProductPopupUpdateComponent,
    UnitTextPipe,
    NzDropDownModule,
    NzMenuModule,
    MenuComponent,
    NzPaginationModule,
  ],
  providers: [DatePipe],
  templateUrl: './product.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./product.component.scss'],
})
export class ProductComponent implements OnInit {
  isLoading = false;
  activeDropdown: any = null;
  listOfData: Product[] = [];
  originalData: Product[] = [];
  listOfCurrentPageData: Product[] = [];
  setOfCheckedId = new Set<string>();
  checked = false;
  indeterminate = false;
  searchKeyword = '';
  isMobile = window.innerWidth < 768;
  selectedItem!: Product;
  isDark = false;
  showPopup = false;
  showPopupCreate = false;
  pageIndex = 1;
  pageSize = 10;
  totalCount = 0;

  @HostListener('window:resize', ['$event'])
  onResize(event: any) {
    this.isMobile = event.target.innerWidth < 768;
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
  }

  constructor(
    private productService: ProductService,
    private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef,
    private modal: NzModalService,
    private toastr: ToastrService,
    private datePipe: DatePipe,
    private location: Location
  ) {}

  get totalPages(): number {
    return Math.ceil(this.totalCount / this.pageSize);
  }

  onRefetch(): void {
    this.fetchData();
  }

  ngOnInit(): void {
    this.fetchData();
  }

  goBack(): void {
    this.location.back();
  }

  toggleDropdown(item: any) {
    this.activeDropdown = this.activeDropdown === item ? null : item;
  }

  closeDropdown() {
    this.activeDropdown = null;
  }

  createProduct() {
    this.showPopupCreate = true;
  }
  viewDetail(item: Product) {
    this.selectedItem = item;
    this.showPopup = true;
  }
  closeProductDetailPopup() {
    this.showPopup = false;
    setTimeout(() => (this.showPopup = false), 300);
  }
  closeProductPopupCreate() {
    this.showPopupCreate = false;
    this.fetchData();
    setTimeout(() => (this.showPopup = false), 300);
  }

  onPageChange(page: number): void {
    this.pageIndex = page;
    this.fetchData(this.pageIndex, this.pageSize);
  }

  fetchData(
    pageIndex: number = this.pageIndex,
    pageSize: number = this.pageSize
  ): void {
    this.isLoading = true;
    this.productService
      .SearchProduct(this.searchKeyword || null, pageSize, pageIndex, undefined)
      .subscribe({
        next: (res) => {
          this.originalData = res.Products || [];
          this.totalCount = res.TotalCount || 0;

          setTimeout(() => {
            this.listOfData = [...this.originalData].sort((a, b) =>
              a.Code.localeCompare(b.Code)
            );

            if (this.isMobile) {
              this.listOfCurrentPageData = [...this.listOfData];
            }
            this.isLoading = false;
            this.cdr.detectChanges();
          });
        },
        error: () => (this.isLoading = false),
      });
  }

  onSearch(): void {
    this.searchKeyword = this.searchKeyword.trim();
    this.fetchData(this.pageIndex, this.pageSize);
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
  }

  listOfSelection = [
    {
      text: 'Chá»n táº¥t cáº£ hÃ ng',
      onSelect: () => {
        this.onAllChecked(true);
      },
    },
    {
      text: 'Chá»n hÃ ng cháºµn',
      onSelect: () => {
        this.listOfCurrentPageData.forEach((data, index) =>
          this.updateCheckedSet(data.Id, index % 2 !== 0)
        );
        this.refreshCheckedStatus();
      },
    },
    {
      text: 'Chá»n hÃ ng láº»',
      onSelect: () => {
        this.listOfCurrentPageData.forEach((data, index) =>
          this.updateCheckedSet(data.Id, index % 2 === 0)
        );
        this.refreshCheckedStatus();
      },
    },
  ];

  updateCheckedSet(id: string, chk: boolean) {
    chk ? this.setOfCheckedId.add(id) : this.setOfCheckedId.delete(id);
  }
  onItemChecked(id: string, chk: boolean) {
    this.updateCheckedSet(id, chk);
    this.refreshCheckedStatus();
  }
  onAllChecked(val: boolean) {
    this.listOfCurrentPageData.forEach((item) =>
      this.updateCheckedSet(item.Id, val)
    );
    this.refreshCheckedStatus();
  }

  onCurrentPageDataChange(data: readonly Product[]): void {
    this.listOfCurrentPageData = [...data];
  }

  refreshCheckedStatus() {
    this.checked = this.listOfCurrentPageData.every((i) =>
      this.setOfCheckedId.has(i.Id)
    );
    this.indeterminate =
      this.listOfCurrentPageData.some((i) => this.setOfCheckedId.has(i.Id)) &&
      !this.checked;
  }
  trackById(index: number, item: Product): string {
    return item.Id;
  }

  private saveAsExcelFile(buffer: any, fileName: string): void {
    const data: Blob = new Blob([buffer], {
      type: 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet;charset=UTF-8',
    });
    saveAs(data, `${fileName}.xlsx`);
  }
  exportToExcel(): void {
    const ws: XLSX.WorkSheet = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([]);
    const header = [
      'MÃ£ sáº£n pháº©m',
      'TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m',
      'Sá»‘ lÆ°á»£ng',
      'ÄÆ¡n vá»‹',
      'NhÃ  cung cáº¥p',
      'MÃ´ táº£',
      'NgÃ y cáº­p nháº­t',
      'Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i',
    ];
    XLSX.utils.sheet_add_aoa(ws, [header], { origin: 'A1' });
    const data = this.listOfData.map((i) => [
      i.Code,
      i.Name,
      i.Quantity,
      i.Name,
      i.SupplierName,
      i.Description || '',
      this.datePipe.transform(i.UpdatedDate, 'dd/MM/yyyy'),
      i.IsActive == false ? 'Hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng' : 'NgÆ°ng hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng',
    ]);
    XLSX.utils.sheet_add_aoa(ws, data, { origin: -1 });
    const wb: XLSX.WorkBook = {
      Sheets: { 'Danh sÃ¡ch sáº£n pháº©m': ws },
      SheetNames: ['Danh sÃ¡ch sáº£n pháº©m'],
    };
    const excelBuffer = XLSX.write(wb, { bookType: 'xlsx', type: 'array' });
    this.saveAsExcelFile(excelBuffer, 'danh_sach_san_pham');
  }

  deleteProduct(item: Product): void {
    this.modal.confirm({
      nzTitle: `Báº¡n cÃ³ cháº¯c muá»‘n xÃ³a sáº£n pháº©m "<b>${item.Name}</b>" nÃ y ?`,
      // nzContent: `<b>${item.Name}</b> sáº½ bá»‹ xÃ³a khá»i há»‡ thá»‘ng.`,
      nzOkText: 'XÃ³a',
      nzCancelText: 'Há»§y',
      nzOnOk: () => {
        this.productService.DeleteProduct(item.Id).subscribe({
          next: () => {
            this.fetchData();
            this.toastr.success('ÄÃ£ xÃ³a thÃ nh cÃ´ng');
          },
          error: (err) => {
            const apiMessage = err.error?.Message;
            let userMessage = 'XÃ³a sáº£n pháº©m tháº¥t báº¡i.';

            if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.APP_MESSAGE.DATA_NOT_EXIST') {
              userMessage = 'Sáº£n pháº©m khÃ´ng tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng.';
            } else if (apiMessage) {
              userMessage = apiMessage;
            }
            this.toastr.error(userMessage);
          },
        });
      },
    });
  }
}


===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product\product.component\services\product-service.ts =====
import { Injectable } from '@angular/core';
import { HttpClient } from '@angular/common/http';
import { Observable } from 'rxjs';
import { Product, ProductReadByIdResponse, ProductResponse } from '../models/product-response.model';
import { ApiUrls } from '../../../../config/api.config';
import { ProductSearchRequest } from '../models/product-search-request.model';
import { ProductCreateRequest } from '../models/product-create-request.model';
import { ProductUpdateRequest } from '../models/product-update-request.model';

@Injectable({ providedIn: 'root' })
export class ProductService {
  constructor(private http: HttpClient) {}

  SearchProduct(
    keySearch: string | null,
    pageSize: number,
    pageIndex: number,
    isActive?: boolean
  ): Observable<ProductResponse> {
    var payload: ProductSearchRequest = {
      keySearch,
      pageIndex,
      pageSize,
      isActive,
    };
    console.log('keyseach: ', keySearch);

    return this.http.post<ProductResponse>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.product.search}`,
      payload
    );
  }

  UpdateProduct(
    Id: string,
    RowVersion: string,
    ProductCategoryId: string,
    Name: string,
    Unit: number,
    IsActive: boolean,
    SalePrice: number,
    ImageUrl?: string,
    SupplierId?: string,
    Description?: string
  ): Observable<Product> {
    const body: ProductUpdateRequest = {
      Id,
      Name,
      ProductCategoryId,
      Unit,
      ImageUrl,
      SupplierId,
      RowVersion,
      IsActive,
      SalePrice,
      Description,
    };
    console.log('payload:', ProductCategoryId);
    return this.http.put<Product>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.product.update}`,
      body
    );
  }

  CreateProduct(
    name: string,
    productCategoryId: string,
    unit: number,
    salePrice: number,
    imageUrl: string,
    description: string,
    isSerialTracked: boolean
  ): Observable<any> {
    const body: ProductCreateRequest = {
      name,
      productCategoryId,
      salePrice,
      unit,
      imageUrl,
      description,
      isSerialTracked
    };
    return this.http.post<any>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.product.create}`,
      body
    );
  }

  DeleteProduct(id: string): Observable<any> {
    return this.http.delete<any>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.product.delete(id)}`
    );
  }
    ReadById(id: string): Observable<ProductReadByIdResponse> {
    return this.http.get<ProductReadByIdResponse>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.product.readById(id)}`
    );
  }
}

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product-category\pages\product-category\product-category.component.ts =====
import { ProductCategoryPopupCreateComponent } from '../product-category-popup-create.component/product-category-popup-create.component';
import { Component, OnInit } from '@angular/core';
import { CommonModule, DatePipe } from '@angular/common';
import { NzTableModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/table';
import { NzCheckboxModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/checkbox';
import { NzButtonModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/button';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { ChangeDetectorRef } from '@angular/core';
import { ProductCategoryService } from '../../services/product-category.service';
import { ProductCategory } from '../../models/product-category-response.model';
import { BottomMenuComponent } from '../../../shared/bottom-menu.component/bottom-menu.component';
import { NzIconModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/icon';
import { HostListener } from '@angular/core';
import { RouterModule } from '@angular/router';
import { ProductCategoryDetailPopup } from '../product-category-detail-popup/product-category-detail-popup';
import { HeaderCommonComponent } from '../../../shared/header-common.component/header-common.component';
import { NzFloatButtonModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/float-button';
import { NzModalModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/modal';
import { NzModalService } from 'ng-zorro-antd/modal';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import * as XLSX from 'xlsx';
import { saveAs } from 'file-saver';
import { Location } from '@angular/common';
import { MenuComponent } from '../../../shared/menu.component/menu.component';

@Component({
  selector: 'product-category',
  standalone: true,
  templateUrl: './product-category.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./product-category.component.scss'],
  imports: [
    CommonModule,
    FormsModule,
    NzTableModule,
    NzCheckboxModule,
    NzButtonModule,
    BottomMenuComponent,
    NzIconModule,
    RouterModule,
    ProductCategoryDetailPopup,
    ProductCategoryPopupCreateComponent,
    HeaderCommonComponent,
    NzModalModule,
    NzFloatButtonModule,
    MenuComponent,
  ],
  providers: [DatePipe],
})
export class ProductCategoryComponent implements OnInit {
  isLoading = false;
  listOfData: ProductCategory[] = [];
  originalData: ProductCategory[] = [];
  listOfCurrentPageData: ProductCategory[] = [];
  setOfCheckedId = new Set<string>();
  checked = false;
  indeterminate = false;
  searchKeyword = '';
  activeDropdown: any = null;
  isMobile = window.innerWidth < 768;
  selectedItem!: ProductCategory;
  pageSize = 10;
  pageIndex = 1;

  @HostListener('window:resize', ['$event'])
  onResize(event: any) {
    this.isMobile = event.target.innerWidth < 768;
  }

  constructor(
    private productService: ProductCategoryService,
    private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef,
    private modal: NzModalService,
    private toastr: ToastrService,
    private datePipe: DatePipe,
    private location: Location
  ) {}
  isDark = false;

  showPopup = false;
  showPopupCreate = false;

  get paginatedList(): ProductCategory[] {
    const start = (this.pageIndex - 1) * this.pageSize;
    return this.listOfData.slice(start, start + this.pageSize);
  }

  toggleDarkMode(): void {
    this.isDark = !this.isDark;
  }

  toggleDropdown(item: any) {
    this.activeDropdown = this.activeDropdown === item ? null : item;
  }

  closeDropdown() {
    this.activeDropdown = null;
  }
  goBack(): void {
    this.location.back();
  }

  onRefetch(): void {
    this.fetchData();
  }

  createProductCategory() {
    this.showPopupCreate = true;
  }

  viewDetail(item: ProductCategory) {
    this.selectedItem = item;
    this.showPopup = true;
  }
  closeProductCategoryDetailPopup() {
    this.showPopup = false;
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.showPopup = false;
    }, 300);
  }

  closeProductCategoryPopupCreate() {
    this.showPopupCreate = false;
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.showPopup = false;
    }, 300);
  }

  ngOnInit(): void {
    this.fetchData();
  }

  fetchData(): void {
    this.isLoading = true;
    this.productService.GetAll().subscribe({
      next: (res) => {
        this.originalData = res.ProductCategories ?? [];
        this.listOfData = [...this.originalData];
        this.isLoading = false;
        console.log('data:', this.listOfData);

        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: () => {
        this.isLoading = false;
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
    });
  }

  onSearch(): void {
    const keyword = this.searchKeyword.trim().toLowerCase();
    this.listOfData = this.originalData.filter(
      (item) =>
        item.Code.toLowerCase().includes(keyword) ||
        item.Name.toLowerCase().includes(keyword)
    );
  }

  listOfSelection = [
    {
      text: 'Chá»n táº¥t cáº£ hÃ ng',
      onSelect: () => {
        this.onAllChecked(true);
      },
    },
    {
      text: 'Chá»n hÃ ng cháºµn',
      onSelect: () => {
        this.listOfCurrentPageData.forEach((data, index) =>
          this.updateCheckedSet(data.Id, index % 2 !== 0)
        );
        this.refreshCheckedStatus();
      },
    },
    {
      text: 'Chá»n hÃ ng láº»',
      onSelect: () => {
        this.listOfCurrentPageData.forEach((data, index) =>
          this.updateCheckedSet(data.Id, index % 2 === 0)
        );
        this.refreshCheckedStatus();
      },
    },
  ];

  updateCheckedSet(id: string, checked: boolean): void {
    checked ? this.setOfCheckedId.add(id) : this.setOfCheckedId.delete(id);
  }

  onItemChecked(id: string, checked: boolean): void {
    this.updateCheckedSet(id, checked);
    this.refreshCheckedStatus();
  }

  onAllChecked(value: boolean): void {
    this.listOfCurrentPageData.forEach((item) =>
      this.updateCheckedSet(item.Id, value)
    );
    this.refreshCheckedStatus();
  }

  onCurrentPageDataChange(data: readonly ProductCategory[]): void {
    this.listOfCurrentPageData = [...data];
    this.refreshCheckedStatus();
  }

  refreshCheckedStatus(): void {
    this.checked = this.listOfCurrentPageData.every((item) =>
      this.setOfCheckedId.has(item.Id)
    );
    this.indeterminate =
      this.listOfCurrentPageData.some((item) =>
        this.setOfCheckedId.has(item.Id)
      ) && !this.checked;
  }

  trackById(index: number, item: ProductCategory): string {
    return item.Id;
  }

  //delete product category
  deleteItem(item: ProductCategory): void {
    this.modal.confirm({
      nzTitle: `Báº¡n cÃ³ cháº¯c muá»‘n xÃ³a loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m "<b>${item.Name}</b>" nÃ y ?`,
      // nzContent: `<b>${item.Name}</b> sáº½ bá»‹ xÃ³a khá»i há»‡ thá»‘ng.`,
      nzOkText: 'XÃ³a',
      nzCancelText: 'Há»§y',
      nzOnOk: () => {
        this.productService.DeleteProductCategory(item.Id).subscribe({
          next: () => {
            this.fetchData();
            this.toastr.success('ÄÃ£ xÃ³a thÃ nh cÃ´ng');
          },
          error: (err) => {
            const apiMessage = err.error?.Message;
            let userMessage = 'XÃ³a loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m tháº¥t báº¡i.';

            if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.APP_MESSAGE.DATA_NOT_EXIST') {
              userMessage = 'Email Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng';
            } else if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.APP_MESSAGE.RECORD_BEING_USED') {
              userMessage = 'Loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘Æ°á»£c sá»­ dá»¥ng.';
            } else if (apiMessage) {
              userMessage = apiMessage;
            }
            this.toastr.error('XÃ³a loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m tháº¥t báº¡i.');
          },
        });
      },
    });
  }

  //export excel
  private saveAsExcelFile(buffer: any, fileName: string): void {
    const data: Blob = new Blob([buffer], {
      type: 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet;charset=UTF-8',
    });
    saveAs(data, `${fileName}.xlsx`);
  }

  exportToExcel(): void {
    const worksheet: XLSX.WorkSheet = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([]);

    // 1. ThÃªm hÃ ng tiÃªu Ä‘á» (header) vá»›i Ä‘á»‹nh dáº¡ng Ä‘áº¹p
    const header = [
      'MÃ£ loáº¡i',
      'TÃªn loáº¡i',
      'MÃ´ táº£',
      'NgÃ y táº¡o',
      'NgÃ y cáº­p nháº­t',
      'Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i',
    ];
    XLSX.utils.sheet_add_aoa(worksheet, [header], { origin: 'A1' });

    // 2. ThÃªm dá»¯ liá»‡u
    const data = this.listOfData.map((item) => [
      item.Code,
      item.Name,
      item.Description,
      this.datePipe.transform(item.CreatedDate, 'dd/MM/yyyy'),
      this.datePipe.transform(item.UpdatedDate, 'dd/MM/yyyy'),
      item.IsActive == false ? 'Hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng' : 'NgÆ°ng hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng',
    ]);
    XLSX.utils.sheet_add_aoa(worksheet, data, { origin: -1 }); // ThÃªm vÃ o sau header

    // 3. Táº¡o workbook
    const workbook: XLSX.WorkBook = {
      Sheets: { 'Danh sÃ¡ch loáº¡i SP': worksheet },
      SheetNames: ['Danh sÃ¡ch loáº¡i SP'],
    };

    // 4. Export
    const excelBuffer = XLSX.write(workbook, {
      bookType: 'xlsx',
      type: 'array',
    });
    this.saveAsExcelFile(excelBuffer, 'danh_sach_loai_san_pham');
  }
}

import { Component, Output, EventEmitter, Input } from '@angular/core';
import { trigger, transition, style, animate } from '@angular/animations';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { ProductCategory } from '../../models/product-category-response.model';
import { ProductCategoryService } from '../../services/product-category.service';
import { finalize } from 'rxjs/operators';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import { NzSelectModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/select';

@Component({
  selector: 'product-category-detail-popup',
  standalone: true,
  imports: [CommonModule, FormsModule, NzSelectModule],
  templateUrl: './product-category-detail-popup.html',
  styleUrl: './product-category-detail-popup.scss',
  animations: [
    trigger('fadeInOut', [
      transition(':enter', [
        style({ opacity: 0, transform: 'scale(0.95)' }),
        animate('300ms ease-out', style({ opacity: 1, transform: 'scale(1)' })),
      ]),
      transition(':leave', [
        animate(
          '200ms ease-in',
          style({ opacity: 0, transform: 'scale(0.95)' })
        ),
      ]),
    ]),
  ],
})
export class ProductCategoryDetailPopup {
  @Input() data!: ProductCategory;
  @Output() closePopup = new EventEmitter<void>();
  @Output() updated = new EventEmitter<void>();
  isClosing = false;
  isSaving = false;

  constructor(
    private productCategoryService: ProductCategoryService,
    private toastr: ToastrService
  ) {}

  close() {
    this.isClosing = true;
    setTimeout(() => this.closePopup.emit(), 200);
  }

  onSubmit() {
    if (this.isSaving) return;
    this.isSaving = true;

    this.productCategoryService
      .UpdateProductCategory(
        this.data.Id,
        this.data.Code.trim(),
        this.data.Name.trim(),
        this.data.RowVersion,
        this.data.IsActive,
        this.data.Description.trim() || ''
      )
      .pipe(finalize(() => (this.isSaving = false)))
      .subscribe({
        next: () => {
          this.toastr.success('Cáº­p nháº­t thÃ nh cÃ´ng');
          this.updated.emit();
          this.close();
        },
        error: (err) => {
          const apiMessage = err.error?.Message;
          let userMessage = 'Cáº­p nháº­t loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m tháº¥t báº¡i.';

          if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.APP_MESSAGE.DATA_NOT_EXIST') {
            userMessage = 'Loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m khÃ´ng tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng.';
          } else if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.APP_MESSAGE.DATA_DUPLICATE') {
            userMessage = 'TÃªn Loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng.';
          } else if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.VALIDATION.MESSAGE.NOT_VALID_ROWVERSION') {
            userMessage = 'Dá»¯ liá»‡u Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Æ°á»£c cáº­p nháº­t bá»Ÿi ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng khÃ¡c. Vui lÃ²ng táº£i láº¡i trang Ä‘á»ƒ tiáº¿p tá»¥c.';
          } else if (apiMessage) {
            userMessage = apiMessage;
          }
          this.toastr.error(userMessage);
        },
      });
  }
}

import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';

import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import { ProductCategoryService } from '../../services/product-category.service';

@Component({
  selector: 'product-category-popup-create',
  imports: [CommonModule, FormsModule],
  templateUrl: './product-category-popup-create.component.html',
  styleUrl: './product-category-popup-create.component.scss',
  animations: [
    trigger('fadeInOut', [
      transition(':enter', [
        style({ opacity: 0, transform: 'scale(0.95)' }),
        animate('300ms ease-out', style({ opacity: 1, transform: 'scale(1)' })),
      ]),
      transition(':leave', [
        animate(
          '200ms ease-in',
          style({ opacity: 0, transform: 'scale(0.95)' })

export class ProductCategoryPopupCreateComponent {
  name: string = '';
  description: string = '';

  @Output() closePopupCreate = new EventEmitter<void>();
  @Output() create = new EventEmitter<void>();
  isClosing = false;
  isSaving = false;

  constructor(
    private productCategoryService: ProductCategoryService,
    private toastr: ToastrService
  ) {}

    this.closePopupCreate.emit();

          this.toastr.success('Táº¡o má»›i loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m thÃ nh cÃ´ng.');
          this.create.emit();
          this.close();
        },
        error: (err) => {
               const apiMessage = err.error?.Message;
        let userMessage = 'Táº¡o má»›i loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m tháº¥t báº¡i.';

        if (apiMessage === 'BACKEND.VALIDATION.MESSAGE.ALREADY_EXIST') {
          userMessage = 'Sáº£n pháº©m loáº¡i sáº£n pháº©m Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng.';
        } else if (apiMessage) {
          userMessage = apiMessage; 
        }
          this.toastr.error(userMessage);

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product-category\services\product-category.service.ts =====
import { CreateProductCategoryRequest } from './../models/product-category-create-request.model';
import { Injectable } from '@angular/core';
import { HttpClient } from '@angular/common/http';
import { Observable } from 'rxjs';
import { ProductCategoryResponse } from '../models/product-category-response.model';
import { ProductCategory } from '../models/product-category-response.model';
import { ProductCategoryUpdateRequest } from '../models/product-category-update-request.model';
import { ApiUrls } from '../../../config/api.config';

@Injectable({ providedIn: 'root' })
export class ProductCategoryService {
  constructor(private http: HttpClient) {}

  GetAll(): Observable<ProductCategoryResponse> {
    return this.http.get<ProductCategoryResponse>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productCategory.getAll}`
    );
  }

  UpdateProductCategory(
    Id: string,
    Code: string,
    Name: string,
    RowVersion: string,
    IsActive: boolean,
    Description: string
  ): Observable<ProductCategory> {
    const body: ProductCategoryUpdateRequest = {
      Id,
      Code,
      Name,
      RowVersion,
      IsActive,
      Description,
    };
    return this.http.put<ProductCategory>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productCategory.update}`,
      body
    );
  }

  CreateProductCategory(name: string, description: string): Observable<any> {
    const body: CreateProductCategoryRequest = {
      name,
      description,
    };
    return this.http.post<any>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productCategory.create}`,
      body
    );
  }

  DeleteProductCategory(id: string): Observable<any> {
    return this.http.delete<any>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productCategory.delete(id)}`
    );
  }
}

}

  ReceiptType: string;

}

export interface ValidateSerialNumberResponse {

  Message: string;
}

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product-item\pages\product-item-import-popup\product-item-import-popup.component.ts =====
import {
  ChangeDetectorRef,
  Component,
  EventEmitter,
  Input,
  OnChanges,
  Output,
  ViewChild,
  ElementRef,
  OnDestroy,
} from '@angular/core';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { NzIconModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/icon';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import { trigger, transition, style, animate } from '@angular/animations';
import { ProductItemService } from '../../services/product-item.service';
import { BrowserMultiFormatReader, IScannerControls } from '@zxing/browser';

@Component({
  selector: 'product-item-import-popup',
  standalone: true,
  imports: [CommonModule, FormsModule, NzIconModule],
  templateUrl: './product-item-import-popup.component.html',
  animations: [
    trigger('fadeInOut', [
      transition(':enter', [
        style({ opacity: 0 }),
        animate('250ms ease-out', style({ opacity: 1 })),
      ]),
      transition(':leave', [
        animate('200ms ease-in', style({ opacity: 0 })),
      ]),
    ]),
  ],
})
export class ProductItemImportPopupComponent
  implements OnChanges, OnDestroy
{
  @Input() visible = false;
  @Input() productId = '';
  @Input() productName = '';
  @Input() importReceiptDetailId?: string;

  @Output() closePopup = new EventEmitter<void>();
  @Output() imported = new EventEmitter<number>();

  @ViewChild('video') video!: ElementRef<HTMLVideoElement>;

  // ===== STATE =====
  snList: string[] = [];
  newSN = '';
  bulkInput = '';
  note = '';

  isSaving = false;
  isClosing = false;
  isScanning = false;

  duplicateInList = false;
  serverDuplicates: string[] = [];

  private codeReader = new BrowserMultiFormatReader();
  private controls?: IScannerControls; // ðŸ”¥ QUAN TRá»ŒNG
  private scannedSet = new Set<string>();
  private lastScanTime = 0;

  constructor(
    private service: ProductItemService,
    private toastr: ToastrService,
    private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef
  ) {}

  // ================= LIFE CYCLE =================

  ngOnChanges(): void {
    if (this.visible) {
      this.reset();
      setTimeout(() => this.startScan(), 300);
    } else {
      this.stopScan();
    }
  }

  ngOnDestroy(): void {
    this.stopScan();
  }

  // ================= CORE =================

  private reset(): void {
    this.snList = [];
    this.newSN = '';
    this.bulkInput = '';
    this.note = '';
    this.duplicateInList = false;
    this.serverDuplicates = [];
    this.isSaving = false;
    this.scannedSet.clear();
    this.lastScanTime = 0;
  }

  addSN(): void {
    const sn = this.newSN.trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!sn) return;

    if (this.snList.includes(sn)) {
      this.duplicateInList = true;
      this.toastr.warning('SN Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i trong danh sÃ¡ch');
      return;
    }

    this.duplicateInList = false;
    this.snList = [...this.snList, sn];
    this.newSN = '';
    this.serverDuplicates = [];

    this.cdr.detectChanges();
  }

  // ================= SCAN =================

  async startScan(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.isScanning) return;

    this.isScanning = true;
    this.cdr.detectChanges();

    try {
      // ðŸ”¥ Ä‘áº£m báº£o khÃ´ng cÃ²n stream cÅ©
      this.stopScan();

      const devices =
        await BrowserMultiFormatReader.listVideoInputDevices();

      if (!devices.length) {
        this.toastr.error('KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y camera');
        this.isScanning = false;
        return;
      }

      const backCamera =
        devices.find((d) =>
          d.label.toLowerCase().includes('back')
        ) || devices[0];

      this.controls = await this.codeReader.decodeFromVideoDevice(
        backCamera.deviceId,
        this.video.nativeElement,
        (result) => {
          if (!result) return;

          const now = Date.now();
          if (now - this.lastScanTime < 500) return;

          const raw = result.getText();
          const sn = this.extractSN(raw);

          if (!sn) return;

          if (this.scannedSet.has(sn)) {
            this.toastr.warning('SN Ä‘Ã£ quÃ©t trÆ°á»›c Ä‘Ã³');
            return;
          }

          this.scannedSet.add(sn);
          this.lastScanTime = now;

          this.newSN = sn;
          this.addSN();

          this.toastr.success('ÄÃ£ quÃ©t: ' + sn);
        }
      );
    } catch (err: any) {
      if (err?.name === 'NotAllowedError') {
        this.toastr.error('Báº¡n Ä‘Ã£ tá»« chá»‘i quyá»n camera');
      } else {
        this.toastr.error('KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ má»Ÿ camera');
      }

      this.isScanning = false;
    }
  }

  stopScan(): void {
    try {
      this.controls?.stop(); // âœ… CHUáº¨N
      this.controls = undefined;
    } catch {}

    this.isScanning = false;
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
  }

  private extractSN(raw: string): string {
    if (!raw) return '';

    raw = raw.trim().toUpperCase();

    const snMatch = raw.match(/SN[:\- ]?([A-Z0-9]+)/);
    if (snMatch) return snMatch[1];

    const serialMatch = raw.match(/SERIAL[:\- ]?([A-Z0-9]+)/);
    if (serialMatch) return serialMatch[1];

    if (/^[A-Z0-9\-]{6,}$/.test(raw)) {
      return raw;
    }

    return '';
  }

  // ================= BULK =================

  addBulk(): void {
    const lines = this.bulkInput
      .split('\n')
      .map((l) => l.trim().toUpperCase())
      .filter((l) => l.length > 0);

    const added: string[] = [];

    lines.forEach((sn) => {
      if (!this.snList.includes(sn) && !added.includes(sn)) {
        added.push(sn);
      }
    });

    this.snList = [...this.snList, ...added];
    this.bulkInput = '';
    this.serverDuplicates = [];

    if (added.length > 0) {
      this.toastr.success(`ÄÃ£ thÃªm ${added.length} serial number`);
    }

    this.cdr.detectChanges();
  }

  removeSN(index: number): void {
    this.snList = this.snList.filter((_, i) => i !== index);
    this.serverDuplicates = [];
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
  }

  clearAll(): void {
    this.snList = [];
    this.serverDuplicates = [];
    this.scannedSet.clear();

    this.cdr.detectChanges();
  }

  // ================= SUBMIT =================

  onSubmit(): void {
    if (this.snList.length === 0 || this.isSaving) return;

    this.isSaving = true;
    this.serverDuplicates = [];

    this.service
      .import({
        productId: this.productId,
        importReceiptDetailId: this.importReceiptDetailId,
        items: this.snList.map((sn) => ({ serialNumber: sn })),
        note: this.note.trim() || undefined,
      })
      .subscribe({
        next: (res) => {
          this.isSaving = false;

          if (res.success) {
            this.toastr.success(
              res.message ||
                `Nháº­p kho thÃ nh cÃ´ng ${res.importedCount} sáº£n pháº©m`
            );
            this.imported.emit(res.importedCount ?? 0);
            this.close();
          } else {
            this.serverDuplicates = res.duplicateSerials ?? [];
            this.toastr.warning(res.message);
          }

          this.cdr.detectChanges();
        },
        error: (err) => {
          this.isSaving = false;

          const msg =
            err.error?.Message ||
            err.error?.message ||
            'Nháº­p kho tháº¥t báº¡i';

          this.toastr.error(msg);
          this.cdr.detectChanges();
        },
      });
  }

  // ================= CLOSE =================

  close(): void {
    this.stopScan();

    this.isClosing = true;
    this.cdr.detectChanges();

    setTimeout(() => {
      this.isClosing = false;
      this.closePopup.emit();
      this.cdr.detectChanges();
    }, 200);
  }
}

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product-item\pages\product-item-list\product-item-list.component.ts =====
// FILE: src/app/features/product-item/pages/product-item-list/product-item-list.component.ts

import {
  ChangeDetectorRef, Component, EventEmitter, HostListener,
  Input, OnChanges, Output,
} from '@angular/core';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { NzTableModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/table';
import { NzPaginationModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/pagination';
import { NzIconModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/icon';
import { trigger, transition, style, animate } from '@angular/animations';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import { ProductItemService } from '../../services/product-item.service';
import {
  ProductItemListDto, ProductItemStatus,
  PRODUCT_ITEM_STATUS_LABEL,
} from '../../models/product-item.model';
import { ProductItemImportPopupComponent } from '../product-item-import-popup/product-item-import-popup.component';
import { ProductItemScanPopupComponent } from '../product-item-scan-popup/product-item-scan-popup.component';

@Component({
  selector: 'product-item-list',
  standalone: true,
  imports: [
    CommonModule,
    FormsModule,
    NzTableModule,
    NzPaginationModule,
    NzIconModule,
    ProductItemImportPopupComponent,
    ProductItemScanPopupComponent,
  ],
  templateUrl: './product-item-list.component.html',
  animations: [
    trigger('fadeInOut', [
      transition(':enter', [
        style({ opacity: 0 }), animate('250ms ease-out', style({ opacity: 1 })),
      ]),
      transition(':leave', [
        animate('200ms ease-in', style({ opacity: 0 })),
      ]),
    ]),
  ],
})
export class ProductItemListComponent implements OnChanges {
  @Input() visible = false;
  @Input() productId = '';
  @Input() productName = '';

  @Output() closePopup = new EventEmitter<void>();

  items: ProductItemListDto[] = [];
  totalCount = 0;
  pageIndex = 1;
  pageSize = 15;
  selectedStatus: number | null = null;

  isLoading = false;
  isClosing = false;
  isMobile = window.innerWidth < 768;

  showImport = false;
  showScan = false;

  @HostListener('window:resize', ['$event'])
  onResize(e: any) {
    this.isMobile = e.target.innerWidth < 768;
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
  }

  constructor(
    private service: ProductItemService,
    private toastr: ToastrService,
    private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef
  ) {}

  ngOnChanges(): void {
    if (this.visible && this.productId) {
      this.pageIndex = 1;
      this.selectedStatus = null;
      this.fetchItems();
    }
  }

  fetchItems(): void {
    if (!this.productId) return;
    this.isLoading = true;

    this.service
      .getByProduct(
        this.productId,
        this.selectedStatus ?? undefined,
        this.pageIndex,
        this.pageSize
      )
      .subscribe({
        next: (res) => {
          this.items = res.Items || [];
          this.totalCount = res.TotalCount || 0;
          this.isLoading = false;
          this.cdr.detectChanges();
        },
        error: () => {
          this.isLoading = false;
          this.toastr.error('KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ táº£i danh sÃ¡ch serial number');
          this.cdr.detectChanges();
        },
      });
  }

  onStatusChange(): void {
    this.pageIndex = 1;
    this.fetchItems();
  }

  onPageChange(page: number): void {
    this.pageIndex = page;
    this.fetchItems();
  }

  openImport(): void {
    this.showImport = true;
  }

  openScan(): void {
    this.showScan = true;
  }

  onImported(count: number): void {
    this.showImport = false;
    this.fetchItems();
    this.toastr.success(`ÄÃ£ nháº­p ${count} serial number vÃ o kho`);
  }

  getStatusLabel(status: ProductItemStatus | string): string {
    return PRODUCT_ITEM_STATUS_LABEL[status as ProductItemStatus] ?? status;
  }

  getStatusBadgeClass(status: ProductItemStatus | string): string {
    const map: Record<string, string> = {
      InStock:   'bg-green-100 text-green-700 dark:bg-green-900 dark:text-green-300',
      Reserved:  'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700 dark:bg-yellow-900 dark:text-yellow-300',
      Sold:      'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 dark:bg-blue-900 dark:text-blue-300',
      Returned:  'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 dark:bg-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300',
      Defective: 'bg-red-100 text-red-700 dark:bg-red-900 dark:text-red-300',
    };
    return map[status as string] ?? '';
  }

  close(): void {
    this.isClosing = true;
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.isClosing = false;
      this.closePopup.emit();
      this.cdr.detectChanges();
    }, 200);
  }
}

            <div class="text-xs text-text-secondary-light dark:text-text-secondary-dark">
              <span *ngIf="tx.FromStatus">{{ getStatusLabel(tx.FromStatus) }} â†’ </span>
              <span [ngClass]="getStatusClass(tx.ToStatus)">{{ getStatusLabel(tx.ToStatus) }}</span>
            </div>
            <div *ngIf="tx.Note" class="text-xs text-neutral-400 mt-0.5">{{ tx.Note }}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Not found -->
    <div
      *ngIf="notFound && !isSearching"
      class="text-center py-10 text-text-secondary-light dark:text-text-secondary-dark"
    >
      <nz-icon nzType="search" nzTheme="outline" class="text-3xl mb-2"></nz-icon>
      <p>KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y sáº£n pháº©m vá»›i serial "{{ lastSearched }}"</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>


===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product-item\pages\product-item-scan-popup\product-item-scan-popup.component.ts =====
// FILE: src/app/features/product-item/pages/product-item-scan-popup/product-item-scan-popup.component.ts

import {
  ChangeDetectorRef, Component, EventEmitter, Input,
  OnChanges, Output,
} from '@angular/core';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { NzIconModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/icon';
import { trigger, transition, style, animate } from '@angular/animations';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import { ProductItemService } from '../../services/product-item.service';
import {
  InventoryTransactionType, ProductItemDto, ProductItemStatus,
  PRODUCT_ITEM_STATUS_COLOR, PRODUCT_ITEM_STATUS_LABEL,
  TransactionHistoryResponse,
} from '../../models/product-item.model';

@Component({
  selector: 'product-item-scan-popup',
  standalone: true,
  imports: [CommonModule, FormsModule, NzIconModule],
  templateUrl: './product-item-scan-popup.component.html',
  animations: [
    trigger('fadeInOut', [
      transition(':enter', [
        style({ opacity: 0 }), animate('250ms ease-out', style({ opacity: 1 })),
      ]),
      transition(':leave', [
        animate('200ms ease-in', style({ opacity: 0 })),
      ]),
    ]),
  ],
})
export class ProductItemScanPopupComponent implements OnChanges {
  @Input() visible = false;
  @Output() closePopup = new EventEmitter<void>();
  @Output() actionDone = new EventEmitter<void>(); // refresh parent list

  inputSN = '';
  lastSearched = '';
  actionNote = '';

  itemDetail: ProductItemDto | null = null;
  history: TransactionHistoryResponse | null = null;
  notFound = false;
  showHistory = false;

  isSearching = false;
  isActioning = false;
  isLoadingHistory = false;
  isClosing = false;

  constructor(
    private service: ProductItemService,
    private toastr: ToastrService,
    private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef
  ) {}

  ngOnChanges(): void {
    if (this.visible) {
      this.resetState();
    }
  }

  private resetState(): void {
    this.inputSN = '';
    this.itemDetail = null;
    this.history = null;
    this.notFound = false;
    this.showHistory = false;
    this.actionNote = '';
    this.isActioning = false;
  }

  search(): void {
    const sn = this.inputSN.trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!sn) return;

    this.lastSearched = sn;
    this.isSearching = true;
    this.itemDetail = null;
    this.history = null;
    this.notFound = false;
    this.showHistory = false;
    this.cdr.detectChanges();

    this.service.getBySN(sn).subscribe({
      next: (res) => {
        this.isSearching = false;
        if (res.Success && res.Item) {
          this.itemDetail = res.Item;
          this.notFound = false;
        } else {
          this.notFound = true;
        }
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: () => {
        this.isSearching = false;
        this.notFound = true;
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
    });
  }

  toggleHistory(): void {
    this.showHistory = !this.showHistory;
    if (this.showHistory && !this.history && this.itemDetail) {
      this.loadHistory(this.itemDetail.SerialNumber);
    }
  }

  private loadHistory(sn: string): void {
    this.isLoadingHistory = true;
    this.service.getHistory(sn).subscribe({
      next: (res) => {
        this.history = res;
        this.isLoadingHistory = false;
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: () => {
        this.isLoadingHistory = false;
        this.toastr.error('KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ táº£i lá»‹ch sá»­');
      },
    });
  }

  onExport(): void {
    if (!this.itemDetail || this.isActioning) return;
    this.isActioning = true;

    this.service.export({
      serialNumber: this.itemDetail.SerialNumber,
      note: this.actionNote.trim() || undefined,
    }).subscribe({
      next: (res) => {
        this.isActioning = false;
        if (res.success) {
          this.toastr.success(res.message || 'Xuáº¥t kho thÃ nh cÃ´ng');
          this.actionDone.emit();
          this.close();
        } else {
          this.toastr.error(res.message);
        }
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: (err) => {
        this.isActioning = false;
        this.toastr.error(err.error?.message || 'Xuáº¥t kho tháº¥t báº¡i');
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
    });
  }

  onReturn(): void {
    if (!this.itemDetail || this.isActioning) return;
    this.isActioning = true;

    this.service.return({
      serialNumber: this.itemDetail.SerialNumber,
      note: this.actionNote.trim() || undefined,
    }).subscribe({
      next: (res) => {
        this.isActioning = false;
        if (res.success) {
          this.toastr.success(res.message || 'Tráº£ hÃ ng thÃ nh cÃ´ng');
          this.actionDone.emit();
          this.close();
        } else {
          this.toastr.error(res.message);
        }
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: (err) => {
        this.isActioning = false;
        this.toastr.error(err.error?.message || 'Tráº£ hÃ ng tháº¥t báº¡i');
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
    });
  }

  onMarkDefective(): void {
    if (!this.itemDetail || this.isActioning) return;
    if (!this.actionNote.trim()) {
      this.toastr.warning('Vui lÃ²ng nháº­p lÃ½ do khi Ä‘Ã¡nh dáº¥u hÃ ng lá»—i');
      return;
    }
    this.isActioning = true;

    this.service.adjust({
      serialNumber: this.itemDetail.SerialNumber,
      targetStatus: 5, // Defective
      note: this.actionNote.trim(),
    }).subscribe({
      next: (res) => {
        this.isActioning = false;
        if (res.success) {
          this.toastr.success('ÄÃ£ Ä‘Ã¡nh dáº¥u hÃ ng lá»—i');
          this.actionDone.emit();
          this.close();
        } else {
          this.toastr.error(res.message);
        }
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: (err) => {
        this.isActioning = false;
        this.toastr.error(err.error?.message || 'Thao tÃ¡c tháº¥t báº¡i');
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
    });
  }

  onRestoreToStock(): void {
    if (!this.itemDetail || this.isActioning) return;
    this.isActioning = true;

    this.service.adjust({
      serialNumber: this.itemDetail.SerialNumber,
      targetStatus: 1, // InStock
      note: this.actionNote.trim() || 'Nháº­p láº¡i kho',
    }).subscribe({
      next: (res) => {
        this.isActioning = false;
        if (res.success) {
          this.toastr.success('ÄÃ£ nháº­p láº¡i kho thÃ nh cÃ´ng');
          this.actionDone.emit();
          this.close();
        } else {
          this.toastr.error(res.message);
        }
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: (err) => {
        this.isActioning = false;
        this.toastr.error(err.error?.message || 'Thao tÃ¡c tháº¥t báº¡i');
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
    });
  }

  // â”€â”€ Helpers â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

  getStatusLabel(status: ProductItemStatus | string): string {
    return PRODUCT_ITEM_STATUS_LABEL[status as ProductItemStatus] ?? status;
  }

  getStatusClass(status: ProductItemStatus | string): string {
    return PRODUCT_ITEM_STATUS_COLOR[status as ProductItemStatus] ?? '';
  }

  getTxTypeLabel(type: InventoryTransactionType): string {
    const map: Record<InventoryTransactionType, string> = {
      Import: 'ðŸ“¥ Nháº­p kho',
      Export: 'ðŸ“¤ Xuáº¥t kho',
      Return: 'â†©ï¸ Tráº£ hÃ ng',
      Adjust: 'âš™ï¸ Äiá»u chá»‰nh',
    };
    return map[type] ?? type;
  }

  getTxTypeClass(type: InventoryTransactionType): string {
    const map: Record<InventoryTransactionType, string> = {
      Import: 'text-success-light dark:text-success-dark',
      Export: 'text-primary-light dark:text-primary-dark',
      Return: 'text-warning-light dark:text-warning-dark',
      Adjust: 'text-info-light dark:text-info-dark',
    };
    return map[type] ?? '';
  }

  close(): void {
    this.isClosing = true;
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.isClosing = false;
      this.closePopup.emit();
      this.cdr.detectChanges();
    }, 200);
  }
}

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product-item\pages\serial-number-scanner\serial-number-scanner.component.ts =====
import {
  Component,
  EventEmitter,
  Input,
  OnDestroy,
  OnInit,
  Output,
  ChangeDetectorRef,
} from '@angular/core';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import { FormsModule } from '@angular/forms';
import { NzModalModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/modal';
import { NzButtonModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/button';
import { NzInputModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/input';
import { NzTableModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/table';
import { NzIconModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/icon';
import { NzTagModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/tag';
import { NzAlertModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/alert';
import { NzSpinModule } from 'ng-zorro-antd/spin';
import { ToastrService } from 'ngx-toastr';
import { Html5Qrcode } from 'html5-qrcode';
import { ProductItemService } from '../../services/product-item.service';

export interface SerialNumberItem {
  serialNumber: string;
  scannedAt: Date;
  status: 'valid' | 'duplicate' | 'invalid' | 'existing';
  message?: string;
}

@Component({
  selector: 'app-serial-number-scanner',
  standalone: true,
  imports: [
    CommonModule,
    FormsModule,
    NzModalModule,
    NzButtonModule,
    NzInputModule,
    NzTableModule,
    NzIconModule,
    NzTagModule,
    NzAlertModule,
    NzSpinModule,
  ],
  templateUrl: './serial-number-scanner.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./serial-number-scanner.component.scss'],
})
export class SerialNumberScannerComponent implements OnInit, OnDestroy {
  @Input() visible = false;
  @Input() productId = '';
  @Input() productName = '';
  @Input() requiredQuantity = 0;
  @Input() existingSerialNumbers: string[] = [];
  
  @Output() visibleChange = new EventEmitter<boolean>();
  @Output() onConfirm = new EventEmitter<string[]>();
  @Output() onCancel = new EventEmitter<void>();

  html5QrCode: Html5Qrcode | null = null;
  isScanning = false;
  isCameraActive = false;
  scannerElementId = 'qr-reader';

  manualSerialNumber = '';
  serialNumbers: SerialNumberItem[] = [];
  
  validCount = 0;
  duplicateCount = 0;
  existingCount = 0;
  isValidating = false;

  private scannedSNSet = new Set<string>();

  constructor(
    private toastr: ToastrService,
    private productItemService: ProductItemService,
    private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef
  ) {}

  ngOnInit(): void {
    this.existingSerialNumbers.forEach(sn => this.scannedSNSet.add(sn.toUpperCase()));
  }

  ngOnDestroy(): void {
    this.stopScanning();
  }

  async startScanning(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      this.html5QrCode = new Html5Qrcode(this.scannerElementId);
      
      await this.html5QrCode.start(
        { facingMode: 'environment' },
        {
          fps: 10,
          qrbox: { width: 250, height: 250 },
        },
        this.onScanSuccess.bind(this),
        this.onScanError.bind(this)
      );

      this.isScanning = true;
      this.isCameraActive = true;
      this.toastr.success('ÄÃ£ báº­t camera. QuÃ©t mÃ£ QR Serial Number');
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error('Camera error:', err);
      this.toastr.error('KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ báº­t camera. Vui lÃ²ng kiá»ƒm tra quyá»n truy cáº­p.');
      this.isScanning = false;
      this.isCameraActive = false;
    }
  }

  async stopScanning(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.html5QrCode && this.isScanning) {
      try {
        await this.html5QrCode.stop();
        this.html5QrCode.clear();
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Stop scanning error:', err);
      } finally {
        this.isScanning = false;
        this.isCameraActive = false;
      }
    }
  }

  private onScanSuccess(decodedText: string, decodedResult: any): void {
    this.addSerialNumber(decodedText.trim());
  }

  private onScanError(errorMessage: string): void {
    // Silent
  }

  addSerialNumber(sn: string): void {
    if (!sn || sn.length === 0) {
      this.toastr.warning('Serial Number khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c Ä‘á»ƒ trá»‘ng');
      return;
    }

    const upperSN = sn.toUpperCase();

    if (this.scannedSNSet.has(upperSN)) {
      this.toastr.warning(`SN "${sn}" Ä‘Ã£ cÃ³ trong danh sÃ¡ch`);
      return;
    }

    const newItem: SerialNumberItem = {
      serialNumber: sn,
      scannedAt: new Date(),
      status: 'valid',
    };

    this.serialNumbers.unshift(newItem);
    this.scannedSNSet.add(upperSN);
    this.updateStats();
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
    this.playBeep();
  }

  addManualSerialNumber(): void {
    const sn = this.manualSerialNumber.trim();
    if (sn) {
      this.addSerialNumber(sn);
      this.manualSerialNumber = '';
    }
  }

  removeSerialNumber(item: SerialNumberItem): void {
    const index = this.serialNumbers.findIndex(
      s => s.serialNumber === item.serialNumber
    );
    if (index > -1) {
      this.serialNumbers.splice(index, 1);
      this.scannedSNSet.delete(item.serialNumber.toUpperCase());
      this.updateStats();
    }
  }

  clearAllSerialNumbers(): void {
    this.serialNumbers = [];
    this.scannedSNSet.clear();
    this.existingSerialNumbers.forEach(sn => this.scannedSNSet.add(sn.toUpperCase()));
    this.updateStats();
  }

  async validateAllSerialNumbers(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.serialNumbers.length === 0) {
      this.toastr.warning('ChÆ°a cÃ³ Serial Number nÃ o Ä‘á»ƒ kiá»ƒm tra');
      return;
    }

    this.isValidating = true;

    const snList = this.serialNumbers.map(s => s.serialNumber);

    this.productItemService.validateSerialNumbers(this.productId, snList).subscribe({
      next: (response) => {
        this.isValidating = false;

        if (response.IsValid) {
          this.toastr.success('Táº¥t cáº£ Serial Number há»£p lá»‡');
        } else {
          const existingSet = new Set(response.ExistingSerialNumbers.map(s => s.toUpperCase()));
          
          this.serialNumbers.forEach(item => {
            if (existingSet.has(item.serialNumber.toUpperCase())) {
              item.status = 'existing';
              item.message = 'SN Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng';
            }
          });

          this.updateStats();
          this.toastr.warning(response.Message || 'CÃ³ SN Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng');
        }
        this.cdr.detectChanges();
      },
      error: (err) => {
        this.isValidating = false;
        this.toastr.error('Lá»—i khi kiá»ƒm tra Serial Number');
        console.error(err);
      },
    });
  }

  private updateStats(): void {
    this.validCount = this.serialNumbers.filter(s => s.status === 'valid').length;
    this.duplicateCount = this.serialNumbers.filter(s => s.status === 'duplicate').length;
    this.existingCount = this.serialNumbers.filter(s => s.status === 'existing').length;
  }

  private playBeep(): void {
    const audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || (window as any).webkitAudioContext)();
    const oscillator = audioContext.createOscillator();
    const gainNode = audioContext.createGain();

    oscillator.connect(gainNode);
    gainNode.connect(audioContext.destination);

    oscillator.frequency.value = 800;
    oscillator.type = 'sine';
    gainNode.gain.value = 0.3;

    oscillator.start(audioContext.currentTime);
    oscillator.stop(audioContext.currentTime + 0.1);
  }

  handleOk(): void {
    const validSNs = this.serialNumbers
      .filter(s => s.status === 'valid')
      .map(s => s.serialNumber);

    if (validSNs.length === 0) {
      this.toastr.warning('KhÃ´ng cÃ³ Serial Number há»£p lá»‡ nÃ o');
      return;
    }

    if (this.requiredQuantity > 0 && validSNs.length !== this.requiredQuantity) {
      this.toastr.warning(
        `YÃªu cáº§u ${this.requiredQuantity} SN, nhÆ°ng chá»‰ cÃ³ ${validSNs.length} SN há»£p lá»‡`
      );
      return;
    }

    this.onConfirm.emit(validSNs);
    this.closeModal();
  }

  handleCancel(): void {
    this.onCancel.emit();
    this.closeModal();
  }

  closeModal(): void {
    this.stopScanning();
    this.visible = false;
    this.visibleChange.emit(false);
  }

  getStatusColor(status: string): string {
    switch (status) {
      case 'valid': return 'green';
      case 'duplicate': return 'orange';
      case 'existing': return 'red';
      case 'invalid': return 'red';
      default: return 'default';
    }
  }

  getStatusText(status: string): string {
    switch (status) {
      case 'valid': return 'Há»£p lá»‡';
      case 'duplicate': return 'TrÃ¹ng láº·p';
      case 'existing': return 'ÄÃ£ tá»“n táº¡i';
      case 'invalid': return 'KhÃ´ng há»£p lá»‡';
      default: return '';
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\product-item\services\product-item.service.ts =====
import { Injectable } from '@angular/core';
import { HttpClient } from '@angular/common/http';
import { Observable } from 'rxjs';
import { ApiUrls } from '../../../config/api.config';
import {
  ProductItem,
  ProductItemImportRequest,
  ProductItemExportRequest,
  ProductItemHistory,
  ValidateSerialNumberResponse,
} from '../models/product-item.model';

@Injectable({
  providedIn: 'root',
})
export class ProductItemService {
  constructor(private http: HttpClient) {}

  /**
   * Láº¥y danh sÃ¡ch sáº£n pháº©m theo ProductId
   */
  getByProduct(productId: string): Observable<ProductItem[]> {
    return this.http.get<ProductItem[]>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productItem.getByProduct}?productId=${productId}`
    );
  }

  /**
   * Láº¥y thÃ´ng tin sáº£n pháº©m theo Serial Number
   */
  getBySN(serialNumber: string): Observable<ProductItem> {
    return this.http.get<ProductItem>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productItem.getBySN(serialNumber)}`
    );
  }

  /**
   * Láº¥y lá»‹ch sá»­ cá»§a má»™t Serial Number
   */
  getHistory(serialNumber: string): Observable<ProductItemHistory[]> {
    return this.http.get<ProductItemHistory[]>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productItem.getHistory(serialNumber)}`
    );
  }

  /**
   * Nháº­p kho vá»›i danh sÃ¡ch Serial Number
   */
  importProductItems(
    request: ProductItemImportRequest
  ): Observable<{ Success: boolean; Message: string }> {
    return this.http.post<{ Success: boolean; Message: string }>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productItem.import}`,
      request
    );
  }

  /**
   * Xuáº¥t kho vá»›i danh sÃ¡ch Serial Number
   */
  exportProductItems(
    request: ProductItemExportRequest
  ): Observable<{ Success: boolean; Message: string }> {
    return this.http.post<{ Success: boolean; Message: string }>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productItem.export}`,
      request
    );
  }

  /**
   * Validate danh sÃ¡ch Serial Number trÆ°á»›c khi nháº­p
   * Kiá»ƒm tra xem cÃ³ SN nÃ o Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i trong há»‡ thá»‘ng chÆ°a
   */
  validateSerialNumbers(
    productId: string,
    serialNumbers: string[]
  ): Observable<ValidateSerialNumberResponse> {
    return this.http.post<ValidateSerialNumberResponse>(
      `${ApiUrls.baseUrl}${ApiUrls.productItem.import}/validate`,
      {
        ProductId: productId,
        SerialNumbers: serialNumbers,
      }
    );
  }
}

===== FILE: D:\BizMate.FE\src\app\features\shared\bottom-menu.component\bottom-menu.component.ts =====
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import { Component } from '@angular/core';
import { Router, RouterModule, NavigationEnd } from '@angular/router';
import { filter } from 'rxjs/operators';

@Component({
  selector: 'bottom-menu',
  standalone: true,
  imports: [CommonModule, RouterModule],
  templateUrl: './bottom-menu.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./bottom-menu.component.scss'],
})
export class BottomMenuComponent {
  active = '';

  menuItems = [
    { id: 'home', icon: 'home', url: '/dashboard' },
    { id: 'fab', icon: 'wrench-screwdriver', url: '/dashboard' },
    { id: 'me', icon: 'user', url: '/user-information' },
  ];

  constructor(private router: Router) {
    // Láº¯ng nghe sá»± kiá»‡n Ä‘á»•i route
    this.router.events
      .pipe(filter(event => event instanceof NavigationEnd))
      .subscribe((event: any) => {
        const current = this.menuItems.find(item =>
          event.urlAfterRedirects.startsWith(item.url)
        );
        this.active = current ? current.id : '';
      });
  }

  setActive(id: string) {
    this.active = id;
  }
}
